{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} void$\ast$ gsasl\+\_\+appinfo\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structGsasl__session}{Gsasl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$}]{sctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+appinfo\+\_\+get\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sctx} & libgsasl session handle.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Retrieve application specific data from libgsasl session handle. The application data is set using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_a5d27f9efaf5a5eb6662fb7366a045841}{gsasl\+\_\+appinfo\+\_\+set()}}. It is normally used by the application to maintain state between the main program and the callback.

Return value\+: Returns the application specific data, or N\+U\+LL.

Deprecated\+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a74333848de28ae2fb05f7bc9532dbd30}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+hook\+\_\+get()}} instead.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gsasl\_base64\_decode()}{gsasl\_base64\_decode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} int gsasl\+\_\+base64\+\_\+decode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char const $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{target,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{targsize }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+base64\+\_\+decode\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em src} & input byte array \\
\hline
{\em target} & output byte array \\
\hline
{\em targsize} & size of output byte array\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Decode Base64 data. Skips all whitespace anywhere. Converts characters, four at a time, starting at (or after) src from Base64 numbers into three 8 bit bytes in the target area.

Return value\+: Returns the number of data bytes stored at the target, or -\/1 on error.

Deprecated\+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{base64_8c_a242baf6a3e3b344fc1d1b6e1c766e198}{gsasl\+\_\+base64\+\_\+from()}} instead. 

Definition at line 1794 of file obsolete.\+c.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} int gsasl\+\_\+base64\+\_\+encode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char const $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{srclength,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{target,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{targsize }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+base64\+\_\+encode\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em src} & input byte array \\
\hline
{\em srclength} & size of input byte array \\
\hline
{\em target} & output byte array \\
\hline
{\em targsize} & size of output byte array\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Encode data as base64. Converts characters, three at a time, starting at src into four base64 characters in the target area until the entire input buffer is encoded.

Return value\+: Returns the number of data bytes stored at the target, or -\/1 on error.

Deprecated\+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{base64_8c_a9cabce698357603f0e19c68b6e26d561}{gsasl\+\_\+base64\+\_\+to()}} instead.

The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & libgsasl handle. \\
\hline
{\em cb} & callback function\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Specify the callback function to use in the client to inform the server of the largest buffer the client is able to receive when using the D\+I\+G\+E\+S\+T-\/\+M\+D5 \char`\"{}auth-\/int\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}auth-\/conf\char`\"{} Quality of Protection (qop). If this directive is missing, the default value 65536 will be assumed. The function can be later retrieved using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_a8bbf3cd2fc9db50f933ae7e3ca7da77e}{gsasl\+\_\+client\+\_\+callback\+\_\+maxbuf\+\_\+get()}}.

Deprecated\+: This function is part of the old callback interface. The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

Specify the callback function to use in the client to know which realm it belongs to. The realm is used by the server to determine which username and password to use. The function can be later retrieved using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_a8b29872e998f8f515b819f14c1ac8fa3}{gsasl\+\_\+client\+\_\+callback\+\_\+realm\+\_\+get()}}.

The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} void gsasl\+\_\+client\+\_\+callback\+\_\+service\+\_\+set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structGsasl}{Gsasl}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl-compat_8h_a6af778833a051dc17fc01643149a9aac}{Gsasl\+\_\+client\+\_\+callback\+\_\+service}}}]{cb }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & libgsasl handle. \\
\hline
{\em cb} & callback function\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Specify the callback function to use in the client to set the name of the service. The service buffer should be a registered G\+S\+S\+A\+PI host-\/based service name, hostname the name of the server. Servicename is used by D\+I\+G\+E\+S\+T-\/\+M\+D5 and should be the name of generic server in case of a replicated service. The function can be later retrieved using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_ac93fe4376a9ecdbbb9d78ae2b7f7035c}{gsasl\+\_\+client\+\_\+callback\+\_\+service\+\_\+get()}}.

Deprecated\+: This function is part of the old callback interface. The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

\index{gsasl\_client\_step@{gsasl\_client\_step}!gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gsasl\_client\_step()}{gsasl\_client\_step()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} int gsasl\+\_\+client\+\_\+step (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structGsasl__session}{Gsasl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$}]{sctx,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{input,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{input\+\_\+len,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{output,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{output\+\_\+len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+client\+\_\+step\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sctx} & libgsasl client handle. \\
\hline
{\em input} & input byte array. \\
\hline
{\em input\+\_\+len} & size of input byte array. \\
\hline
{\em output} & output byte array. \\
\hline
{\em output\+\_\+len} & size of output byte array.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Perform one step of S\+A\+SL authentication in client. This reads data from server (specified with input and input\+\_\+len), processes it (potentially invoking callbacks to the application), and writes data to server (into variables output and output\+\_\+len).

The contents of the output buffer is unspecified if this functions returns anything other than G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+N\+E\+E\+D\+S\+\_\+\+M\+O\+RE.

Return value\+: Returns G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+OK if authenticated terminated successfully, G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+N\+E\+E\+D\+S\+\_\+\+M\+O\+RE if more data is needed, or error code.

Deprecated\+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a0a3dcfe02502ecadd6484ff1181e1924}{gsasl\+\_\+step()}} instead. 

Definition at line 163 of file obsolete.\+c.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{gsasl-compat_8h_abc94ff8463dd90bd0de3d39cd478efe7}\label{gsasl-compat_8h_abc94ff8463dd90bd0de3d39cd478efe7}} 
\index{gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}!gsasl\_md5pwd\_get\_password@{gsasl\_md5pwd\_get\_password}}
\index{gsasl\_md5pwd\_get\_password@{gsasl\_md5pwd\_get\_password}!gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gsasl\_md5pwd\_get\_password()}{gsasl\_md5pwd\_get\_password()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} int gsasl\+\_\+md5pwd\+\_\+get\+\_\+password (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{username,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{key,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{keylen }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+md5pwd\+\_\+get\+\_\+password\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em filename} & filename of file containing passwords. \\
\hline
{\em username} & username string. \\
\hline
{\em key} & output character array. \\
\hline
{\em keylen} & input maximum size of output character array, on output contains actual length of output array.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Retrieve password for user from specified file. To find out how large the output array must be, call this function with out=N\+U\+LL.

The file should be on the UoW \char`\"{}\+M\+D5 Based Authentication\char`\"{} format, which means it is in text format with comments denoted by \# first on the line, with user entries looking as \char`\"{}username\+T\+A\+Bpassword\char`\"{}. This function removes CR and LF at the end of lines before processing. T\+AB, CR, and LF denote A\+S\+C\+II values 9, 13, and 10, respectively.

Return value\+: Return G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+OK if output buffer contains the password, G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+E\+N\+T\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR if the user could not be found, or other error code.

Deprecated\+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_ad4ed7472e5992d92b0e8327fdc96239d}{gsasl\+\_\+simple\+\_\+getpass()}} instead. 

Definition at line 1687 of file obsolete.\+c.

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & libgsasl handle. \\
\hline
{\em cb} & callback function\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Specify the callback function to use in the server to inform the client of the cipher suites supported. The D\+ES and 3D\+ES ciphers must be supported for interoperability. It is currently used by the D\+I\+G\+E\+S\+T-\/\+M\+D5 mechanism. The function can be later retrieved using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_a8d73dd09113439e109e7ab17abbcdb4c}{gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+cipher\+\_\+get()}}.

Deprecated\+: This function is part of the old callback interface. The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & libgsasl handle. \\
\hline
{\em cb} & callback function\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Specify the callback function to use in the server for checking if a G\+S\+S\+A\+PI user is authorized for username (by, e.\+g., calling krb5\+\_\+userok()). The function should return G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+OK if the user should be permitted access, or an error code such as G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+E\+N\+T\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR on failure. The function can be later retrieved using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_aebd925eb089f69a31f72fb3d44f8fc3f}{gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+gssapi\+\_\+get()}}.

Deprecated\+: This function is part of the old callback interface. The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

Specify the callback function to use in the server to inform the client of the largest buffer the server is able to receive when using the D\+I\+G\+E\+S\+T-\/\+M\+D5 \char`\"{}auth-\/int\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}auth-\/conf\char`\"{} Quality of Protection (qop). The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gsasl\_server\_callback\_realm\_set()}{gsasl\_server\_callback\_realm\_set()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} void gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+realm\+\_\+set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structGsasl}{Gsasl}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl-compat_8h_aef39cc72c54b3cb124d26c791bb129b0}{Gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+realm}}}]{cb }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+realm\+\_\+set\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & libgsasl handle. \\
\hline
{\em cb} & callback function\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Specify the callback function to use in the server to know which realm it serves. The realm is used by the user to determine which username and password to use. The function can be later retrieved using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_aa4cd3736d6bae5fe36f5383241d1a7dd}{gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+realm\+\_\+get()}}.

Deprecated\+: This function is part of the old callback interface. The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties. 

Definition at line 1275 of file obsolete.\+c.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gsasl\_server\_callback\_securid\_set()}{gsasl\_server\_callback\_securid\_set()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} void gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+securid\+\_\+set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structGsasl}{Gsasl}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl-compat_8h_a101c03588d22076866b9d4d2acbcde46}{Gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+securid}}}]{cb }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+securid\+\_\+set\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & libgsasl handle. \\
\hline
{\em cb} & callback function\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Specify the callback function to use in the server for validating a user via the S\+E\+C\+U\+R\+ID mechanism. The function should return G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+OK if user authenticated successfully, G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+U\+R\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+E\+E\+D\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+I\+T\+I\+O\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+S\+S\+C\+O\+DE if it wants another passcode, G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+U\+R\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+E\+E\+D\+\_\+\+N\+E\+W\+\_\+\+P\+IN if it wants a P\+IN change, or an error. When (and only when) G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+U\+R\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+E\+E\+D\+\_\+\+N\+E\+W\+\_\+\+P\+IN is returned, suggestpin can be populated with a P\+IN code the server suggests, and suggestpinlen set to the length of the P\+IN. The function can be later retrieved using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_aff3544f97453e3738bd4ab36883c15fb}{gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+securid\+\_\+get()}}.

Deprecated\+: This function is part of the old callback interface. The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties. 

Definition at line 1443 of file obsolete.\+c.

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & libgsasl handle. \\

{\em cb} & callback function\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Specify the callback function to use in the server to set the name of the service. The service buffer should be a registered G\+S\+S\+A\+PI host-\/based service name, hostname the name of the server. The function can be later retrieved using \mbox{\hyperlink{obsolete_8c_aac2890fb0123fe02ed29e935c839b6d2}{gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+callback\+\_\+service\+\_\+get()}}.

The new interface uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_a35a03c3e0e6b5a17674fae51d42f02fe}{gsasl\+\_\+callback\+\_\+set()}} to set the application callback, and uses \mbox{\hyperlink{callback_8c_abf495dc11359ec995c2a3bf3ba310ad4}{gsasl\+\_\+callback()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_aa0cae2a9a9cfc284d771fc98b72b92ec}{gsasl\+\_\+property\+\_\+get()}} to invoke the callback for certain properties.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{gsasl-compat_8h_abf3d003a8798eeef596138330e4ef144}\label{gsasl-compat_8h_abf3d003a8798eeef596138330e4ef144}} 
\index{gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}!gsasl\_server\_step@{gsasl\_server\_step}}
\index{gsasl\_server\_step@{gsasl\_server\_step}!gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gsasl\_server\_step()}{gsasl\_server\_step()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} int gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+step (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structGsasl__session}{Gsasl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$}]{sctx,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{input,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{input\+\_\+len,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{output,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{output\+\_\+len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+server\+\_\+step\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sctx} & libgsasl server handle. \\
\hline
{\em input} & input byte array. \\
\hline
{\em input\+\_\+len} & size of input byte array. \\
\hline
{\em output} & output byte array. \\
\hline
{\em output\+\_\+len} & size of output byte array.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Perform one step of S\+A\+SL authentication in server. This reads data from client (specified with input and input\+\_\+len), processes it (potentially invoking callbacks to the application), and writes data to client (into variables output and output\+\_\+len).

The contents of the output buffer is unspecified if this functions returns anything other than G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+N\+E\+E\+D\+S\+\_\+\+M\+O\+RE.

Return value\+: Returns G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+OK if authenticated terminated successfully, G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+N\+E\+E\+D\+S\+\_\+\+M\+O\+RE if more data is needed, or error code.

Deprecated\+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a0a3dcfe02502ecadd6484ff1181e1924}{gsasl\+\_\+step()}} instead. 

Definition at line 193 of file obsolete.\+c.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{gsasl-compat_8h_a4bf7264790f6f73140e24d46aa15cebd}\label{gsasl-compat_8h_a4bf7264790f6f73140e24d46aa15cebd}} 
\index{gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}!gsasl\_stringprep\_nfkc@{gsasl\_stringprep\_nfkc}}
\index{gsasl\_stringprep\_nfkc@{gsasl\_stringprep\_nfkc}!gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gsasl\_stringprep\_nfkc()}{gsasl\_stringprep\_nfkc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} char$\ast$ gsasl\+\_\+stringprep\+\_\+nfkc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{in,  }\item[{ssize\+\_\+t}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+stringprep\+\_\+nfkc\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em in} & a U\+T\+F-\/8 encoded string. \\
\hline
{\em len} & length of @str, in bytes, or -\/1 if @str is nul-\/terminated.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Converts a string into canonical form, standardizing such issues as whether a character with an accent is represented as a base character and combining accent or as a single precomposed character.

The normalization mode is N\+F\+KC (A\+LL C\+O\+M\+P\+O\+SE). It standardizes differences that do not affect the text content, such as the above-\/mentioned accent representation. It standardizes the \char`\"{}compatibility\char`\"{} characters in Unicode, such as S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+S\+C\+R\+I\+PT T\+H\+R\+EE to the standard forms (in this case D\+I\+G\+IT T\+H\+R\+EE). Formatting information may be lost but for most text operations such characters should be considered the same. It returns a result with composed forms rather than a maximally decomposed form.

Return value\+: Return a newly allocated string, that is the N\+F\+KC normalized form of @str, o N\+U\+LL on error.

Deprecated\+: No replacement functionality in G\+NU S\+A\+SL, use G\+NU Libidn instead. Note that in S\+A\+SL, you most likely want to use S\+A\+S\+Lprep and not bare N\+F\+KC, see \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_af30e2a33d1f3b6da519750754c339468}{gsasl\+\_\+saslprep()}}. 

Definition at line 1581 of file obsolete.\+c.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{gsasl-compat_8h_aea90a07b7da9d2807293d3e0de464b25}\label{gsasl-compat_8h_aea90a07b7da9d2807293d3e0de464b25}} 
\index{gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}!gsasl\_stringprep\_saslprep@{gsasl\_stringprep\_saslprep}}
\index{gsasl\_stringprep\_saslprep@{gsasl\_stringprep\_saslprep}!gsasl-\/compat.h@{gsasl-\/compat.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gsasl\_stringprep\_saslprep()}{gsasl\_stringprep\_saslprep()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_a9456922879452d4e57ae9c017b56da36}{G\+S\+A\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} char$\ast$ gsasl\+\_\+stringprep\+\_\+saslprep (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{in,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{stringprep\+\_\+rc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

gsasl\+\_\+stringprep\+\_\+saslprep\+: 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em in} & input A\+S\+C\+II or U\+T\+F-\/8 string with data to prepare according to S\+A\+S\+Lprep. \\
\hline
{\em stringprep\+\_\+rc} & pointer to output variable with stringprep error code, or N\+U\+LL to indicate that you don\textquotesingle{}t care about it.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Process a Unicode string for comparison, according to the \char`\"{}\+S\+A\+S\+Lprep\char`\"{} stringprep profile. This function is intended to be used by Simple Authentication and Security Layer (S\+A\+SL) mechanisms (such as P\+L\+A\+IN, C\+R\+A\+M-\/\+M\+D5, and D\+I\+G\+E\+S\+T-\/\+M\+D5) as well as other protocols exchanging user names and/or passwords.

Return value\+: Return a newly allocated string that is the \char`\"{}\+S\+A\+S\+Lprep\char`\"{} processed form of the input string, or N\+U\+LL on error, in which case @stringprep\+\_\+rc contain the stringprep library error code.

Deprecated\+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{gsasl_8h_af30e2a33d1f3b6da519750754c339468}{gsasl\+\_\+saslprep()}} instead. 

Definition at line 1612 of file obsolete.\+c.
